  document.getElementById('lousaOutput').innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--text-light);"><div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px;">🖊️</div><div>Cole texto ou imagem e clique em Organizar</div></div>';
}

// ===================== CAIXA DOS SÓCIOS — INBOX + KANBAN =====================
let tasks = [];
let inboxFilter = 'todos';

function setInboxFilter(filter) {
  inboxFilter = filter;
  ['todos','Leonardo','Nívio','Marcelo'].forEach(f => {
    const btn = document.getElementById('inboxFilter_' + f);
    if (!btn) return;
    if (f === filter) {
      btn.style.background = f === 'todos' ? 'var(--orange)' : (f === 'Leonardo' ? '#E65100' : f === 'Nívio' ? '#00695C' : '#4527A0');
      btn.style.color = '#fff';
    } else {
      btn.style.background = '#fff';
      btn.style.color = f === 'Leonardo' ? '#E65100' : f === 'Nívio' ? '#00695C' : f === 'Marcelo' ? '#4527A0' : 'var(--orange)';
    }
  });
  renderInbox();
}

async function loadTasks() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/tasks');
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error();
    tasks = await res.json();
    // migrate legacy status values
    tasks = tasks.map(t => {
      if (t.status === 'pending') return {...t, status: 'recente'};
      if (t.status === 'done')    return {...t, status: 'respondido'};
      return t;
    });
    renderInbox();
    renderKanban();
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Erro ao carregar tasks:', err);
  }
}

function renderTasks() { renderKanban(); renderInbox(); }

// ---- INBOX ----
const USER_COLORS = {
  Jackeline: { bg:'#FCE4EC', color:'#E91E63' },
  Pedro:     { bg:'#E3F2FD', color:'#1565C0' },
  Claudio:   { bg:'#E8F5E9', color:'#2E7D32' },
  Stella:    { bg:'#F3E5F5', color:'#6A1B9A' },
  Leonardo:  { bg:'#FBE9E7', color:'#E65100' },
  Nívio:     { bg:'#E0F2F1', color:'#00695C' },
  Marcelo:   { bg:'#EDE7F6', color:'#4527A0' },
};

function renderInbox() {
  const list = document.getElementById('inboxList');
  if (!list) return;
  const sorted = [...tasks].sort((a, b) => b.ts - a.ts);
  const unread = sorted.filter(t => !t.read).length;
  const badge = document.getElementById('inboxUnreadBadge');
  if (badge) badge.textContent = unread > 0 ? unread : '0';

  const filtered = inboxFilter === 'todos' ? sorted : sorted.filter(t => t.socio === inboxFilter);

  if (filtered.length === 0) {
    const msg = inboxFilter === 'todos'
      ? 'Nenhuma mensagem ainda.<br>Escreva uma ou mencione um socio no chat.'
      : `Nenhuma mensagem para ${inboxFilter} ainda.`;
    list.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px 16px;color:var(--text-light);font-size:11px;"><div style="font-size:28px;margin-bottom:8px;">📭</div>${msg}</div>`;
    return;
  }

  const prioStyle = { alta:'background:#FFEBEE;color:var(--red);', media:'background:#FFF8E1;color:#F57F17;', normal:'background:var(--green-light);color:var(--green);' };
  const typeIcon  = { manual:'✉️', mention:'🤖' };

  const socioColors = { Leonardo:'#E65100', 'Nívio':'#00695C', Marcelo:'#4527A0' };

  list.innerHTML = filtered.map(t => {
    const uc  = USER_COLORS[t.from] || { bg:'#f0f0f0', color:'#555' };
    const ini = (t.from||'?').slice(0,2).toUpperCase();
    const dt  = _fmtTime(t.ts);
    const preview = (t.details||'').slice(0, 55) + ((t.details||'').length > 55 ? '…' : '');
    const prio = prioStyle[t.priority] || prioStyle.normal;
    const unreadCls = !t.read ? 'unread' : '';
    const icon = typeIcon[t.type] || '✉️';
    const respBadge = t.respondido_por
      ? `<span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:800;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:10px;background:${socioColors[t.respondido_por]||'#555'};color:#fff;margin-left:6px;">Respondido por ${t.respondido_por}</span>`
      : '';
    const respBtns = t.status !== 'respondido'
      ? `<button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:#E8F5E9;color:#2E7D32;border:1px solid #A5D6A7;" onclick="responderTask(${t.ts},'Leonardo');event.stopPropagation()">✓ Leonardo</button>
         <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:#E0F2F1;color:#00695C;border:1px solid #80CBC4;" onclick="responderTask(${t.ts},'Nívio');event.stopPropagation()">✓ Nívio</button>
         <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:#EDE7F6;color:#4527A0;border:1px solid #B39DDB;" onclick="responderTask(${t.ts},'Marcelo');event.stopPropagation()">✓ Marcelo</button>`
      : `<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--green);font-weight:700;">Resolvido</span>`;
    return `
      <div class="inbox-item ${unreadCls}" id="inbox_${t.ts}" onclick="openInboxItem(${t.ts})">
        <div class="inbox-avatar" style="background:${uc.bg};color:${uc.color};">${ini}</div>
        <div class="inbox-meta">
          <div class="inbox-from-row">
            <span class="inbox-from">${icon} ${t.from}</span>
            <span class="inbox-time">${dt}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="inbox-subject">${t.subject}
            <span class="inbox-priority" style="${prio}">${t.priority?.toUpperCase()}</span>
            ${respBadge}
          </div>
          <div class="inbox-preview">Para: ${t.socio} · ${preview}</div>
        </div>
        ${!t.read ? '<div class="inbox-unread-dot"></div>' : ''}
      </div>
      <div class="inbox-detail" id="detail_${t.ts}">
        <div style="font-size:11px;line-height:1.8;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:10px;">${(t.details||'').replace(/\n/g,'<br>')}</div>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap;align-items:center;">
          ${respBtns}
          ${t.status==='recente'?`<button class="btn btn-gray btn-sm" onclick="moveTask(${t.ts},'afazer');event.stopPropagation()">→ A Fazer</button>`:''}
          <button class="btn btn-gray btn-sm" onclick="deleteTask(${t.ts});event.stopPropagation()">Apagar</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function openInboxItem(ts) {
  // Mark as read
  const task = tasks.find(t => t.ts === ts);
  if (task && !task.read) {
    task.read = true;
    fetch('/api/tasks', { method:'PATCH', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ ts, read: true }) });
  }

  // Toggle detail panel
  const detail = document.getElementById('detail_' + ts);
  const item   = document.getElementById('inbox_' + ts);
  if (!detail) return;
  const isOpen = detail.classList.contains('open');
  // Close all open details first
  document.querySelectorAll('.inbox-detail.open').forEach(d => d.classList.remove('open'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.inbox-item.expanded').forEach(i => i.classList.remove('expanded'));
  if (!isOpen) {
    detail.classList.add('open');
    item?.classList.add('expanded');
  }
  // Update unread badge
  const unread = tasks.filter(t => !t.read).length;
  const badge = document.getElementById('inboxUnreadBadge');
  if (badge) badge.textContent = unread > 0 ? unread : '0';
  // Remove unread dot from this item
  item?.classList.remove('unread');
  item?.querySelector('.inbox-unread-dot')?.remove();
}

function toggleCompose() {
  const panel = document.getElementById('composePanel');
  const btn   = document.getElementById('btnCompose');
  if (!panel) return;
  const open = panel.classList.toggle('open');
  if (btn) btn.textContent = open ? '✕ Fechar' : '✏️ Escrever';
  if (open) document.getElementById('taskFrom')?.focus();
}

function _fmtTime(ts) {
  const d = new Date(ts);
  const now = new Date();
  const diffH = (now - d) / 3600000;
  if (diffH < 24 && d.getDate() === now.getDate())
    return d.toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR', { hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit' });
  if (diffH < 48) return 'Ontem';
  return d.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', { day:'2-digit', month:'2-digit' });
}

// Auto-detect sócio mentions in chat and create inbox items
function detectChatMention(userMsg, chatUserName) {
  const socios = ['leonardo','nívio','nivio','marcelo'];
  const socioMap = { leonardo:'Leonardo', 'nívio':'Nívio', nivio:'Nívio', marcelo:'Marcelo' };
  const lower = userMsg.toLowerCase();
  const triggerWords = ['avisar','falar com','perguntar','@','precisa','preciso','pode ver','ver com','verificar com','perguntar para','precisa de','precisaria','ajuda','chamar','acionar','envolver','passar para','repassar','consultar','informar','notificar','escalona','escalar','reportar','comunicar','alertar','saber disso','saber sobre','resolver isso','aprovar','autorizar','decidir'];
  const hasTrigger = triggerWords.some(w => lower.includes(w));
  if (!hasTrigger) return;

  for (const s of socios) {
    if (lower.includes(s)) {
      const name = socioMap[s];
      const subject = userMsg.slice(0, 60) + (userMsg.length > 60 ? '…' : '');
      const newTask = {
        ts: Date.now(),
        type: 'mention',
        socio: name,
        from: chatUserName,
        subject: `Menção no chat: ${subject}`,
        details: userMsg,
        priority: 'normal',
        status: 'recente',
        read: false
      };
      tasks.unshift(newTask);
      fetch('/api/tasks', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify(newTask) });
      renderInbox();
      renderKanban();
      showToast(`🤖 Mensagem criada para ${name} a partir do chat`);
      break;
    }
  }
}

function renderKanban() {
  const recentes   = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'recente').sort((a,b) => b.ts - a.ts);
  const afazer     = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'afazer').sort((a,b) => b.ts - a.ts);
  const respondidos = tasks.filter(t => t.status === 'respondido').sort((a,b) => b.ts - a.ts);

  _setCount('cnt_recentes', recentes.length);
  _setCount('cnt_afazer', afazer.length);
  _setCount('cnt_respondidos', respondidos.length);

  _renderOperadoresCol('col_recentes', recentes, true, 'Nenhuma mensagem nova');
  _renderOperadoresCol('col_afazer', afazer, true, 'Tudo em dia');
  _renderOperadoresCol('col_respondidos', respondidos, false, 'Nenhum ainda');
}

function _setCount(id, n) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.textContent = n;
}

function _renderOperadoresCol(colId, items, showActions, emptyMsg) {
  const col = document.getElementById(colId);
  if (!col) return;
  if (items.length === 0) { col.innerHTML = `<div class="kanban-empty">${emptyMsg}</div>`; return; }

  const prioBadges = { alta: '#FFEBEE', media: '#FFF8E1', normal: 'var(--green-light)' };
  const prioText   = { alta: 'var(--red)', media: '#F57F17', normal: 'var(--green)' };
  const socioColors = { Leonardo: '#E65100', 'Nívio': '#00695C', Marcelo: '#4527A0' };

  col.innerHTML = items.map(t => {
    const respBadge = t.respondido_por
      ? `<span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:800;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:10px;background:${socioColors[t.respondido_por]||'#555'};color:#fff;">Respondido por ${t.respondido_por}</span>`
      : '';
    const actionBtns = showActions ? `
      <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;margin-top:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
        ${t.status==='recente' ? `<button class="btn btn-gray btn-sm" onclick="moveTask(${t.ts},'afazer')">→ A Fazer</button>` : ''}
        <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:#E8F5E9;color:#2E7D32;border:1px solid #A5D6A7;" onclick="responderTask(${t.ts},'Leonardo')">✓ Leonardo</button>
        <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:#E0F2F1;color:#00695C;border:1px solid #80CBC4;" onclick="responderTask(${t.ts},'Nívio')">✓ Nívio</button>
        <button class="btn btn-sm" style="background:#EDE7F6;color:#4527A0;border:1px solid #B39DDB;" onclick="responderTask(${t.ts},'Marcelo')">✓ Marcelo</button>
      </div>` : '';
    return `
    <div class="kanban-card p-${t.priority}">
      <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;gap:4px;margin-bottom:6px;">
        <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap;align-items:center;">
          <span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:800;padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px;background:${prioBadges[t.priority]||'#eee'};color:${prioText[t.priority]||'#555'};">${t.priority?.toUpperCase()}</span>
          <span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:800;padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px;background:var(--orange-light);color:var(--orange);">${t.socio}</span>
          ${respBadge}
        </div>
        <button onclick="deleteTask(${t.ts})" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:#ccc;font-size:14px;line-height:1;flex-shrink:0;">✕</button>
      </div>
      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:3px;">${t.subject}</div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-light);margin-bottom:6px;">De: <strong>${t.from}</strong> · ${new Date(t.ts).toLocaleString('pt-BR',{day:'2-digit',month:'2-digit',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})}</div>
      <div style="font-size:11px;line-height:1.6;color:var(--text);">${t.details}</div>
      ${actionBtns}
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function addTask() {
  const socio    = document.getElementById('taskSocio').value;
  const from     = document.getElementById('taskFrom').value.trim();
  const subject  = document.getElementById('taskSubject').value.trim();
  const details  = document.getElementById('taskDetails').value.trim();
  const priority = document.getElementById('taskPriority').value;
  if (!from || !subject || !details) { showToast('⚠️ Preencha De, Assunto e Detalhes!'); return; }
  const newTask = { ts: Date.now(), type: 'manual', socio, from, subject, details, priority, status: 'recente', read: false };
  tasks.unshift(newTask);
  fetch('/api/tasks', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify(newTask) });
  document.getElementById('taskFrom').value = '';
  document.getElementById('taskSubject').value = '';
  document.getElementById('taskDetails').value = '';
  toggleCompose();
  renderInbox();
  renderKanban();
  showToast(`✅ Mensagem enviada para ${socio}!`);
}

function moveTask(ts, newStatus) {
  tasks = tasks.map(t => t.ts === ts ? {...t, status: newStatus} : t);
  fetch('/api/tasks', { method:'PATCH', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ ts, status: newStatus }) });
  renderInbox();
  renderKanban();
  const labels = { afazer: 'A Fazer', respondido: 'Respondido' };
  showToast(`Movido para ${labels[newStatus] || newStatus}`);
}

function responderTask(ts, socio) {
  tasks = tasks.map(t => t.ts === ts ? {...t, status: 'respondido', respondido_por: socio} : t);
  fetch('/api/tasks', { method:'PATCH', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ ts, status: 'respondido', respondido_por: socio }) });
  renderInbox();
  renderKanban();
  showToast(`${socio} marcou como respondido`);
}

function doneTask(ts) { moveTask(ts, 'respondido'); }

function deleteTask(ts) {
  tasks = tasks.filter(t => t.ts !== ts);
  fetch(`/api/tasks?ts=${ts}`, { method:'DELETE' });
  renderInbox();
  renderKanban();
}

// ---- GESTORES: auto-linked com tratativas da equipe ----
async function loadGestoresKanban() {
  const colPending = document.getElementById('col_emandamento');
  const colDone    = document.getElementById('col_finalizadas');
  if (!colPending || !colDone) return;

  colPending.innerHTML = '<div class="kanban-empty">Carregando...</div>';
  colDone.innerHTML    = '<div class="kanban-empty">Carregando...</div>';

  const teamUsers = ['Jackeline','Pedro','Claudio','Stella'];
  try {
    const all = (await Promise.all(teamUsers.map(async u => {
      try {
        const r = await fetch(`/api/history?user=${encodeURIComponent(u)}`);
        const d = await r.json();
        return Array.isArray(d) ? d : [];
      } catch { return []; }
    }))).flat().sort((a,b) => new Date(b.updated_at) - new Date(a.updated_at));

    const pending = all.filter(c => c.status !== 'ok');
    const done    = all.filter(c => c.status === 'ok').slice(0, 30);

    _setCount('cnt_emandamento', pending.length);
    _setCount('cnt_finalizadas', done.length);

    _renderGestoresCol(colPending, pending, true);
    _renderGestoresCol(colDone, done, false);
  } catch(err) {
    colPending.innerHTML = `<div class="kanban-empty" style="color:var(--red);">Erro: ${err.message}</div>`;
    colDone.innerHTML    = '<div class="kanban-empty">—</div>';
  }
}

function _renderGestoresCol(container, convs, isPending) {
  if (convs.length === 0) {
    container.innerHTML = `<div class="kanban-empty">${isPending ? 'Nenhuma pendência 🎉' : 'Nenhuma finalizada ainda'}</div>`;
    return;
  }
  const userColors = { Jackeline:'#E91E63', Pedro:'#1565C0', Claudio:'#2E7D32', Stella:'#6A1B9A' };
  container.innerHTML = convs.map(c => {
    const dt = new Date(c.updated_at).toLocaleString('pt-BR',{day:'2-digit',month:'2-digit',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
    const uc = userColors[c.user_name] || 'var(--orange)';
    const safeName = (c.user_name||'').replace(/'/g,'');
    const safeContact = (c.contact_name||'').replace(/'/g,'&#39;');
    return `<div class="kanban-card auto-card">
      <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:6px;">
        <span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:800;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:4px;background:${uc};color:#fff;">${c.user_name}</span>
        <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-light);">${dt}</span>
      </div>
      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:2px;">${c.contact_name || 'Sem contato identificado'}</div>
      <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${c.title || '—'}</div>
      ${isPending ? `<button class="btn btn-orange btn-sm" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px;" onclick="cobrarOperador('${safeName}','${safeContact}')">📢 Cobrar ${c.user_name}</button>` : ''}
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function cobrarOperador(nome, contato) {
  const msg = `Lembrete copiado! Cole no WhatsApp:\n"${nome}, o card do contato "${contato}" ainda está em aberto. Pode dar um update?"`;
  const text = `${nome}, o card do contato "${contato}" ainda está em aberto. Pode dar um update?`;
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => showToast(`📋 Mensagem copiada — cole no WhatsApp para ${nome}!`));
}

// ===================== ANONIMIZADOR =====================
// ===================== ANONIMIZADOR =====================
let anonCanvas, anonCtx, anonImg, anonDrawing = false, anonStart = {};
let anonPdfDoc = null, anonPdfCurrentPage = 1, anonCurrentFileName = 'documento';

// --- Drag & Drop ---
function anonDragOver(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  const z = document.getElementById('anonDropZone');
  z.style.borderColor = 'var(--orange)';
  z.style.background = 'var(--orange-light)';
}
function anonDragLeave(e) {
  const z = document.getElementById('anonDropZone');
  z.style.borderColor = '';
  z.style.background = '';
}
function anonDrop(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  anonDragLeave(e);
  const file = e.dataTransfer?.files?.[0];
  if (file) loadAnonFile(file);
}

function handleAnonPaste(e) {
  const items = e.clipboardData?.items;
  if (!items) return;
  for (const item of items) {
    if (item.type.startsWith('image/')) {
      const blob = item.getAsFile();
      loadAnonFile(blob);
      return;
    }
  }
}

function handleAnonFile(input) {
  const file = input.files[0];
  if (file) loadAnonFile(file);
  input.value = '';
}

function loadAnonFile(file) {
  anonCurrentFileName = file.name.replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '') || 'documento';
  if (file.type === 'application/pdf' || file.name.endsWith('.pdf')) {
    loadAnonPdf(file);
  } else {
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = ev => loadAnonImage(ev.target.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    document.getElementById('anonPdfNav').style.display = 'none';
    anonPdfDoc = null;
  }
}

// --- PDF via PDF.js ---
async function loadAnonPdf(file) {
  if (!window.pdfjsLib) {
    showToast('Carregando PDF.js...', 'warn');
    await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.min.js';
      s.onload = resolve; s.onerror = reject;
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });
    window.pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc =
      'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.worker.min.js';
  }
  const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
  anonPdfDoc = await window.pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: arrayBuffer }).promise;
  anonPdfCurrentPage = 1;
  await renderAnonPdfPage(anonPdfCurrentPage);
  const nav = document.getElementById('anonPdfNav');
  nav.style.display = anonPdfDoc.numPages > 1 ? 'flex' : 'none';
  updateAnonPdfLabel();
}

async function renderAnonPdfPage(pageNum) {
  const page = await anonPdfDoc.getPage(pageNum);
  const viewport = page.getViewport({ scale: 2 });
  const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');
  offscreen.width = viewport.width;
  offscreen.height = viewport.height;
  await page.render({ canvasContext: offscreen.getContext('2d'), viewport }).promise;
  loadAnonImage(offscreen.toDataURL('image/png'));
}

async function anonPdfPage(delta) {
  if (!anonPdfDoc) return;
  const next = anonPdfCurrentPage + delta;
  if (next < 1 || next > anonPdfDoc.numPages) return;
  document.querySelectorAll('.anon-rect').forEach(r => r.remove());
  anonPdfCurrentPage = next;
  await renderAnonPdfPage(anonPdfCurrentPage);
  updateAnonPdfLabel();
}

function updateAnonPdfLabel() {
  document.getElementById('anonPdfLabel').textContent =
    `Pág ${anonPdfCurrentPage}/${anonPdfDoc?.numPages || 1}`;
}

// --- Canvas ---
function _anonCoords(e) {
  const r = anonCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  // Corrige a diferença entre tamanho CSS e pixels reais do canvas
  const scaleX = anonCanvas.width / r.width;
  const scaleY = anonCanvas.height / r.height;
  return {
    x: (e.clientX - r.left) * scaleX,
    y: (e.clientY - r.top) * scaleY,
  };
}

function _redrawAnon() {
  if (!anonImg) return;
  anonCtx.drawImage(anonImg, 0, 0, anonCanvas.width, anonCanvas.height);
  document.querySelectorAll('.anon-rect').forEach(rect => {
    anonCtx.fillStyle = '#000';
    anonCtx.fillRect(+rect.dataset.x, +rect.dataset.y, +rect.dataset.w, +rect.dataset.h);
  });
}

function loadAnonImage(src) {
  const wrapper = document.getElementById('anonCanvasWrapper');
  wrapper.style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('anonHint').style.display = 'none';
  anonCanvas = document.getElementById('anonCanvas');
  anonCtx = anonCanvas.getContext('2d');
  anonImg = new Image();
  anonImg.onload = () => {
    anonCanvas.width = anonImg.width;
    anonCanvas.height = anonImg.height;
    anonCtx.drawImage(anonImg, 0, 0);
    showToast('Documento carregado. Arraste para cobrir áreas sensíveis.');
  };
  anonImg.src = src;

  anonCanvas.onmousedown = e => {
    anonDrawing = true;
    anonStart = _anonCoords(e);
  };
  anonCanvas.onmousemove = e => {
    if (!anonDrawing) return;
    const { x, y } = _anonCoords(e);
    _redrawAnon();
    anonCtx.strokeStyle = '#000'; anonCtx.lineWidth = 2; anonCtx.setLineDash([5, 3]);
    anonCtx.strokeRect(anonStart.x, anonStart.y, x - anonStart.x, y - anonStart.y);
  };
  anonCanvas.onmouseup = e => {
    if (!anonDrawing) return;
    anonDrawing = false;
    anonCtx.setLineDash([]);
    const { x, y } = _anonCoords(e);
    const w = x - anonStart.x, h = y - anonStart.y;
    if (Math.abs(w) < 4 || Math.abs(h) < 4) { _redrawAnon(); return; }
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'anon-rect';
    div.dataset.x = anonStart.x; div.dataset.y = anonStart.y;
    div.dataset.w = w; div.dataset.h = h;
    document.getElementById('anonRects').appendChild(div);
    anonCtx.fillStyle = '#000';
    anonCtx.fillRect(anonStart.x, anonStart.y, w, h);
  };
  anonCanvas.onmouseleave = () => {
    if (anonDrawing) { anonDrawing = false; anonCtx.setLineDash([]); _redrawAnon(); }
  };
}

function desfazerAnon() {
  const rects = document.querySelectorAll('.anon-rect');
  if (!rects.length) return;
  rects[rects.length - 1].remove();
  _redrawAnon();
}

async function downloadAnon() {
  if (!anonCanvas) return;
  const dataUrl = anonCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
  const filename = `${anonCurrentFileName}_anonimizado.png`;
  const sizeKb = Math.round(dataUrl.length * 0.75 / 1024);

  // Dispara o download imediatamente
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.download = filename;
  link.href = dataUrl;
  link.click();

  // Thumbnail pequeno para listagem
  const thumb = document.createElement('canvas');
  thumb.width = 120;
  thumb.height = Math.round(120 * anonCanvas.height / anonCanvas.width);
  thumb.getContext('2d').drawImage(anonCanvas, 0, 0, thumb.width, thumb.height);
  const thumbData = thumb.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.6);

  try {
    await fetch('/api/anonimizar', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        filename,
        thumb: thumbData,
        dataUrl,
        size_kb: sizeKb,
        user_name: window.SAMBA_USER?.name || window.SAMBA_USER?.email || '',
      })
    });
    renderAnonLibrary();
    showToast('Download iniciado e salvo na biblioteca!');
  } catch {
    showToast('Download feito, mas erro ao salvar na biblioteca.', 'warn');
  }
}

async function renderAnonLibrary() {
  const container = document.getElementById('anonLibrary');
  if (!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);text-align:center;padding:10px;">Carregando...</div>';
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/anonimizar');
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error();
    const items = await res.json();

    if (!items.length) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);text-align:center;padding:10px;">Nenhum arquivo gerado ainda.</div>';
      return;
    }

    container.innerHTML = items.map(item => {
      const date = new Date(item.created_at).toLocaleString('pt-BR', {day:'2-digit',month:'2-digit',year:'2-digit',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
      const user = item.user_name ? ` · ${item.user_name}` : '';
      const sizeLabel = item.size_kb ? ` · ${item.size_kb > 1024 ? (item.size_kb/1024).toFixed(1)+'MB' : item.size_kb+'KB'}` : '';
      return `
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:8px;padding:8px 10px;">
        <img src="${item.thumb}" style="width:48px;height:auto;border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);flex-shrink:0;">
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
          <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap;">${item.filename}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-light);">${date}${user}${sizeLabel}</div>
        </div>
        <button onclick="downloadAnonById('${item._id}','${item.filename}')" style="background:var(--orange);color:#fff;border:none;border-radius:6px;padding:4px 10px;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;flex-shrink:0;">⬇️</button>
        <button onclick="deleteAnonLib('${item._id}',this)" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;color:var(--text-light);flex-shrink:0;">✕</button>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  } catch {
    container.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--red);text-align:center;padding:10px;">Erro ao carregar biblioteca.</div>';
  }
}

async function downloadAnonById(id, filename) {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`/api/anonimizar?id=${id}`);
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error();
    const item = await res.json();
    if (!item.dataUrl) { showToast('Arquivo muito grande para re-download. Refaça a anonimização.', 'warn'); return; }
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.download = filename;
    link.href = item.dataUrl;
    link.click();
  } catch {
    showToast('Erro ao baixar arquivo.', 'warn');
  }
}

async function deleteAnonLib(id, btn) {
  btn.closest('div[style]').style.opacity = '0.4';
  try {
    await fetch(`/api/anonimizar?id=${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' });
    renderAnonLibrary();
  } catch {
    showToast('Erro ao excluir.', 'warn');
    btn.closest('div[style]').style.opacity = '1';
  }
}

function limparAnon() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.anon-rect').forEach(r => r.remove());
  document.getElementById('anonCanvasWrapper').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('anonHint').style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('anonPdfNav').style.display = 'none';
  anonImg = null; anonCanvas = null; anonCtx = null; anonPdfDoc = null;
}
</script>
</body>
</html>


notion-route.js:

// =====================================================================
// ROTA: POST /api/notion
// Adicione este trecho no seu servidor Express (server.js / index.js)
// =====================================================================
//
// CONFIGURAÇÃO:
// 1. Crie uma integração em: https://www.notion.so/my-integrations
// 2. Copie o token "secret_xxxx..."
// 3. Defina a variável de ambiente: NOTION_TOKEN=secret_xxxx...
//    (ou coloque direto em NOTION_TOKEN abaixo para teste)
//
// 4. No Notion, abra o CRM "CRM - Leads LinkedIn"
//    → Clique em "..." no canto superior direito → Connections → Add → selecione sua integração
//
// 5. Adicione no seu package.json se ainda não tiver:
//    npm install @notionhq/client
// =====================================================================

const { Client } = require('@notionhq/client');

const NOTION_TOKEN = process.env.NOTION_TOKEN || 'SEU_TOKEN_AQUI';
const notion = new Client({ auth: NOTION_TOKEN });

// Adicione esta rota no seu app Express:
app.post('/api/notion', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { parent, pages } = req.body;

    if (!parent?.data_source_id || !pages?.length) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Payload inválido' });
    }

    const pageData = pages[0];
    const props = pageData.properties || {};

    // Monta as properties no formato da Notion API
    const notionProperties = {};

    // Título obrigatório
    notionProperties['Nome do Lead'] = {
      title: [{ text: { content: props['Nome do Lead'] || 'Lead sem nome' } }]
    };

    // Campos de texto
    const textFields = ['Empresa','Cargo','Pais','Volume Mencionado','Porto Destino','Observacoes','Proximo Passo'];
    for (const field of textFields) {
      if (props[field]) {
        notionProperties[field] = { rich_text: [{ text: { content: String(props[field]) } }] };
      }
    }

    // URL
    if (props['Perfil LinkedIn']) {
      notionProperties['Perfil LinkedIn'] = { url: props['Perfil LinkedIn'] };
    }

    // Select fields
    if (props['Status']) {
      notionProperties['Status'] = { select: { name: props['Status'] } };
    }
    if (props['Perfil']) {
      notionProperties['Perfil'] = { select: { name: props['Perfil'] } };
    }
    if (props['Responsavel']) {
      notionProperties['Responsavel'] = { select: { name: props['Responsavel'] } };
    }

    // Multi-select: Commodity de Interesse
    if (props['Commodity de Interesse']) {
      const commodities = JSON.parse(props['Commodity de Interesse']);
      notionProperties['Commodity de Interesse'] = {
        multi_select: commodities.map(name => ({ name }))
      };
    }

    // Datas
    if (props['date:Data Primeiro Contato:start']) {
      notionProperties['Data Primeiro Contato'] = {
        date: { start: props['date:Data Primeiro Contato:start'] }
      };
    }
    if (props['date:Data Ultimo Contato:start']) {
      notionProperties['Data Ultimo Contato'] = {
        date: { start: props['date:Data Ultimo Contato:start'] }
      };
    }

    const response = await notion.pages.create({
      parent: { database_id: parent.data_source_id },
      properties: notionProperties,
    });

    res.json({ url: response.url, id: response.id });

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Notion API error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({
      error: 'Erro ao salvar no Notion',
      message: error.message
    });
  }
});


Daqui pra baixo dentro da pasta api:

_auth.js:

import { createHmac } from 'crypto';

const COOKIE = 'samba_auth';

export function getAuthCookie(req) {
  const header = req.headers.cookie || '';
  for (const part of header.split(';')) {
    const [k, ...rest] = part.trim().split('=');
    if (k.trim() === COOKIE) return decodeURIComponent(rest.join('='));
  }
  return null;
}

export function signToken(payload) {
  const data = Buffer.from(JSON.stringify(payload)).toString('base64url');
  const sig = createHmac('sha256', process.env.JWT_SECRET).update(data).digest('base64url');
  return `${data}.${sig}`;
}

export function verifyToken(token) {
  if (!token || typeof token !== 'string') return null;
  const dot = token.lastIndexOf('.');
  if (dot < 0) return null;
  const data = token.slice(0, dot);
  const sig = token.slice(dot + 1);
  const expected = createHmac('sha256', process.env.JWT_SECRET).update(data).digest('base64url');
  if (sig !== expected) return null;
  try {
    const payload = JSON.parse(Buffer.from(data, 'base64url').toString('utf8'));
    if (!payload.exp || payload.exp < Date.now()) return null;
    return payload;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

export function requireAuth(req, res) {
  const token = getAuthCookie(req);
  const user = verifyToken(token);
  if (!user) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: 'Não autenticado' });
    return null;
  }
  return user;
}

export function cookieHeader(token) {
  const secure = process.env.VERCEL_ENV === 'production' ? '; Secure' : '';
  if (!token) return `${COOKIE}=; Path=/; HttpOnly${secure}; SameSite=Lax; Max-Age=0`;
  return `${COOKIE}=${token}; Path=/; HttpOnly${secure}; SameSite=Lax; Max-Age=28800`;
}


anonimizar.js:

import { MongoClient, ObjectId, ServerApiVersion } from 'mongodb';
import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const clientOptions = {
  serverApi: { version: ServerApiVersion.v1, strict: false, deprecationErrors: false },
  tls: true,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 10000,
  connectTimeoutMS: 10000,
};

let cachedClient = null;

async function getClient() {
  if (cachedClient?.topology?.isConnected()) return cachedClient;
  cachedClient = null;
  const client = new MongoClient(process.env.MONGODB_URI, clientOptions);
  await client.connect();
  cachedClient = client;
  return client;
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, DELETE, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();

  try {
    const client = await getClient();
    const db = client.db('samba');
    const col = db.collection('anonimizados');

    // GET — listar (sem dataUrl para não sobrecarregar)
    if (req.method === 'GET') {
      const { id } = req.query;

      if (id) {
        const item = await col.findOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) }, { projection: { dataUrl: 1, filename: 1 } });
        if (!item) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Não encontrado' });
        return res.status(200).json(item);
      }

      const items = await col
        .find({}, { projection: { dataUrl: 0 } }) // exclui dataUrl da listagem
        .sort({ created_at: -1 })
        .limit(50)
        .toArray();
      return res.status(200).json(items);
    }

    // POST — salvar arquivo anonimizado
    if (req.method === 'POST') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      const { filename, thumb, dataUrl, user_name, size_kb } = body;

      if (!filename || !thumb) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'filename e thumb obrigatórios' });

      // Verifica tamanho — dataUrl pode ser grande; MongoDB limita 16MB por doc
      const estimatedSize = (dataUrl?.length || 0) * 0.75; // base64 → bytes
      const doc = {
        filename,
        thumb,
        user_name: user_name || '',
        size_kb: size_kb || 0,
        created_at: new Date(),
        // Só salva o dataUrl completo se couber (~10MB margin)
        ...(estimatedSize < 10_000_000 ? { dataUrl } : {}),
      };

      const result = await col.insertOne(doc);
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true, id: result.insertedId.toString() });
    }

    // DELETE
    if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
      const { id } = req.query;
      if (!id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'id obrigatório' });
      await col.deleteOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) });
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Método não permitido' });

  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: err.message });
  }
}


claude.js:

import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  // Permitir apenas POST
  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return res.status(405).json({ error: "Método não permitido" });
  }

  try {
    // 🔥 Garante que o body vem certo (Vercel às vezes manda string)
    const body = typeof req.body === "string"
      ? JSON.parse(req.body)
      : req.body;

    // 🔥 Validação básica
    if (!body || !body.messages) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: "Body inválido. 'messages' é obrigatório."
      });
    }

    // 🔥 Chamada para Anthropic
    const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "x-api-key": process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY,
        "anthropic-version": "2023-06-01"
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(body)
    });

    // 🔥 Pega resposta bruta
    const data = await response.json();

    // 🔴 Se a API retornou erro, repassa corretamente
    if (!response.ok) {
      return res.status(response.status).json({
        error: data.error?.message || "Erro na API da Anthropic",
        full: data
      });
    }

    // 🔥 Extrai texto da resposta (garante compatibilidade)
    const text =
      data?.content?.map(c => c.text).join("") ||
      "Sem resposta da IA";

    // ✅ Retorna padrão simplificado pro frontend
    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      text,
      raw: data
    });

  } catch (err) {
    console.error("Erro no backend:", err);

    return res.status(500).json({
      error: "Erro interno no servidor",
      message: err.message
    });
  }
}


crm.js:

import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const DATABASE_ID = '2a6a74bf-1f21-460d-8e0b-d0cd0779f84a';
const NOTION_QUERY = `https://api.notion.com/v1/databases/${DATABASE_ID}/query`;

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();
  if (req.method !== 'GET') return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Metodo nao permitido' });

  const token = process.env.NOTION_TOKEN;
  if (!token) return res.status(500).json({ error: 'NOTION_TOKEN nao configurado' });

  try {
    const { filter, sort, search } = req.query;

    const body = {
      page_size: 100,
      sorts: [{ property: 'Data Ultimo Contato', direction: 'descending' }],
    };

    // Filtro por status
    const filters = [];
    if (filter && filter !== 'todos') {
      filters.push({ property: 'Status', select: { equals: filter } });
    }
    // Busca por nome/empresa
    if (search) {
      filters.push({
        or: [
          { property: 'Nome do Lead', title: { contains: search } },
          { property: 'Empresa', rich_text: { contains: search } },
        ]
      });
    }
    if (filters.length === 1) body.filter = filters[0];
    else if (filters.length > 1) body.filter = { and: filters };

    const response = await fetch(NOTION_QUERY, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Notion-Version': '2022-06-28',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(body),
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      const err = await response.json();
      return res.status(502).json({ error: err.message || 'Erro na API do Notion' });
    }

    const data = await response.json();

    const leads = data.results.map(page => {
      const p = page.properties;
      return {
        id: page.id,
        url: page.url,
        nome:          p['Nome do Lead']?.title?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        empresa:       p['Empresa']?.rich_text?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        cargo:         p['Cargo']?.rich_text?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        pais:          p['Pais']?.rich_text?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        status:        p['Status']?.select?.name || '',
        perfil:        p['Perfil']?.select?.name || '',
        responsavel:   p['Responsavel']?.select?.name || '',
        commodity:     p['Commodity de Interesse']?.multi_select?.map(c => c.name).join(', ') || '',
        volume:        p['Volume Mencionado']?.rich_text?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        porto:         p['Porto Destino']?.rich_text?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        proximo_passo: p['Proximo Passo']?.rich_text?.[0]?.plain_text || '',
        email:         p['Email']?.email || '',
        telefone:      p['Telefone']?.phone_number || '',
        mobile:        p['Mobile']?.phone_number || '',
        linkedin:      p['Perfil LinkedIn']?.url || '',
        ncda:          p['NCDA Assinado']?.checkbox || false,
        whatsapp:      p['WhatsApp Criado']?.checkbox || false,
        como_chegou:   p['Como Chegou']?.select?.name || '',
        data_primeiro: p['Data Primeiro Contato']?.date?.start || '',
        data_ultimo:   p['Data Ultimo Contato']?.date?.start || '',
      };
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ leads, total: leads.length });

  } catch (error) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: error.message });
  }
}


diligencia.js:

import { MongoClient, ObjectId, ServerApiVersion } from 'mongodb';
import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const clientOptions = {
  serverApi: { version: ServerApiVersion.v1, strict: false, deprecationErrors: false },
  tls: true,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 10000,
  connectTimeoutMS: 10000,
};

let cachedClient = null;

async function getClient() {
  if (cachedClient?.topology?.isConnected()) return cachedClient;
  cachedClient = null;
  const client = new MongoClient(process.env.MONGODB_URI, clientOptions);
  await client.connect();
  cachedClient = client;
  return client;
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, DELETE, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();

  try {
    const client = await getClient();
    const db = client.db('samba');
    const col = db.collection('due_diligence');

    // GET — listar histórico
    if (req.method === 'GET') {
      const { id } = req.query;

      if (id) {
        const item = await col.findOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) });
        if (!item) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Não encontrado' });
        return res.status(200).json(item);
      }

      const items = await col
        .find({}, { projection: { input_text: 0, result: 0 } })
        .sort({ created_at: -1 })
        .limit(50)
        .toArray();
      return res.status(200).json(items);
    }

    // POST — salvar análise
    if (req.method === 'POST') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      const { entidade, pais, score, nivel_risco, avancar, result, input_text, user_name } = body;

      if (!entidade || !result) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Parâmetros inválidos' });
      }

      const doc = {
        entidade,
        pais: pais || '',
        score: score ?? null,
        nivel_risco: nivel_risco || '',
        avancar: avancar !== false,
        result,
        input_text: input_text || '',
        user_name: user_name || '',
        created_at: new Date(),
      };

      const inserted = await col.insertOne(doc);
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true, id: inserted.insertedId.toString() });
    }

    // DELETE — remover análise
    if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
      const { id } = req.query;
      if (!id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'id obrigatório' });
      await col.deleteOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) });
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Método não permitido' });

  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: err.message });
  }
}


faqs.js:

import { MongoClient, ObjectId, ServerApiVersion } from 'mongodb';
import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const clientOptions = {
  serverApi: { version: ServerApiVersion.v1, strict: false, deprecationErrors: false },
  tls: true,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 10000,
  connectTimeoutMS: 10000,
};

let cachedClient = null;

async function getClient() {
  if (cachedClient?.topology?.isConnected()) return cachedClient;
  cachedClient = null;
  const client = new MongoClient(process.env.MONGODB_URI, clientOptions);
  await client.connect();
  cachedClient = client;
  return client;
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, DELETE, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();

  try {
    const client = await getClient();
    const db = client.db('samba');
    const col = db.collection('faqs');

    // GET — listar FAQs salvas
    if (req.method === 'GET') {
      const items = await col
        .find({})
        .sort({ created_at: -1 })
        .limit(100)
        .toArray();
      return res.status(200).json(items);
    }

    // POST — salvar FAQ
    if (req.method === 'POST') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      const { question, answer, user_name } = body;
      if (!question || !answer) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'question e answer obrigatórios' });
      const doc = { question, answer, user_name: user_name || '', created_at: new Date() };
      const result = await col.insertOne(doc);
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true, id: result.insertedId.toString() });
    }

    // DELETE — remover FAQ
    if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
      const { id } = req.query;
      if (!id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'id obrigatório' });
      await col.deleteOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) });
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Método não permitido' });

  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: err.message });
  }
}

history.js:

import { MongoClient, ObjectId, ServerApiVersion } from 'mongodb';
import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const clientOptions = {
  serverApi: { version: ServerApiVersion.v1, strict: false, deprecationErrors: false },
  tls: true,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 10000,
  connectTimeoutMS: 10000,
};

let cachedClient = null;

async function getClient() {
  if (cachedClient?.topology?.isConnected()) return cachedClient;
  cachedClient = null;
  const client = new MongoClient(process.env.MONGODB_URI, clientOptions);
  await client.connect();
  cachedClient = client;
  return client;
}

async function extractContactInfo(messages) {
  const textSample = messages
    .map(m => `${m.role === 'user' ? 'Usuário' : 'IA'}: ${m.content}`)
    .join('\n')
    .slice(0, 4000);

  try {
    const res = await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'x-api-key': process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY,
        'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01'
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: 'claude-haiku-4-5-20251001',
        max_tokens: 150,
        messages: [{
          role: 'user',
          content: `Analise esta conversa e retorne SOMENTE um JSON:
{"contact_name": "nome do lead/contato/pessoa mencionada em qualquer idioma (não o nome do funcionário da Samba), ou null se não encontrado", "follow_up_date": "data de follow-up/próximo contato no formato YYYY-MM-DD, ou null", "status": "ok se a conversa indica que foi resolvido/feito/concluído/done, senão pending"}

Conversa:
${textSample}

JSON:`
        }]
      })
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    const raw = data?.content?.[0]?.text || '{}';
    return JSON.parse(raw.replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim());
  } catch {
    return { contact_name: null, follow_up_date: null, status: 'pending' };
  }
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, PATCH, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');

  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();

  try {
    const client = await getClient();
    const db = client.db('samba');
    const col = db.collection('conversations');

    // GET — buscar por ID ou listar por usuário
    if (req.method === 'GET') {
      const { user, id } = req.query;

      if (id) {
        const conv = await col.findOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) });
        if (!conv) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Conversa não encontrada' });
        return res.status(200).json(conv);
      }

      if (user) {
        const convs = await col
          .find({ user_name: user }, { projection: { messages: 0 } })
          .sort({ updated_at: -1 })
          .limit(30)
          .toArray();
        return res.status(200).json(convs);
      }

      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Parâmetro user ou id obrigatório' });
    }

    // POST — criar ou atualizar conversa
    if (req.method === 'POST') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      const { action, conversation_id, user_name, messages, force_status } = body;

      if (action !== 'save' || !user_name || !messages) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Parâmetros inválidos' });
      }

      const now = new Date();

      if (conversation_id) {
        const existing = await col.findOne(
          { _id: new ObjectId(conversation_id) },
          { projection: { contact_name: 1, status: 1 } }
        );
        const updateFields = { messages, updated_at: now };

        if (force_status) {
          updateFields.status = force_status;
        } else {
          const needsExtraction = !existing?.contact_name || existing?.status === 'pending';
          if (needsExtraction) {
            const extracted = await extractContactInfo(messages);
            if (extracted.contact_name) updateFields.contact_name = extracted.contact_name;
            if (extracted.follow_up_date) updateFields.follow_up_date = extracted.follow_up_date;
            if (extracted.status === 'ok') updateFields.status = 'ok';
          }
        }

        await col.updateOne({ _id: new ObjectId(conversation_id) }, { $set: updateFields });
        return res.status(200).json({ success: true, conversation_id });

      } else {
        const firstUserMsg = messages.find(m => m.role === 'user')?.content || 'Nova conversa';
        const title = firstUserMsg.slice(0, 80) + (firstUserMsg.length > 80 ? '...' : '');
        const extracted = await extractContactInfo(messages);

        const result = await col.insertOne({
          user_name,
          title,
          contact_name: extracted.contact_name || null,
          follow_up_date: extracted.follow_up_date || null,
          status: force_status || extracted.status || 'pending',
          started_at: now,
          updated_at: now,
          messages
        });
        return res.status(200).json({ success: true, conversation_id: result.insertedId.toString() });
      }
    }

    // PATCH — atualizar nome, data ou status manualmente
    if (req.method === 'PATCH') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      const { id, contact_name, follow_up_date, status } = body;

      if (!id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'id obrigatório' });

      const updateFields = { updated_at: new Date() };
      if (contact_name !== undefined) updateFields.contact_name = contact_name || null;
      if (follow_up_date !== undefined) updateFields.follow_up_date = follow_up_date || null;
      if (status !== undefined) updateFields.status = status;

      await col.updateOne({ _id: new ObjectId(id) }, { $set: updateFields });
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Método não permitido' });

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Erro em /api/history:', err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: err.message });
  }
}

notion.js:

import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const DATABASE_ID = '2a6a74bf-1f21-460d-8e0b-d0cd0779f84a';
const NOTION_API = 'https://api.notion.com/v1/pages';
const NOTION_QUERY = `https://api.notion.com/v1/databases/${DATABASE_ID}/query`;

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();
  if (req.method !== 'POST') return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Metodo nao permitido' });

  const token = process.env.NOTION_TOKEN;
  if (!token) return res.status(500).json({ error: 'NOTION_TOKEN nao configurado' });

  try {
    const { pages } = req.body;
    if (!pages?.length) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Payload invalido' });

    const props = pages[0].properties || {};
    const notionProps = {};

    notionProps['Nome do Lead'] = {
      title: [{ text: { content: props['Nome do Lead'] || 'Lead sem nome' } }]
    };

    const textFields = ['Empresa', 'Cargo', 'Pais', 'Volume Mencionado', 'Porto Destino', 'Observacoes', 'Proximo Passo'];
    for (const field of textFields) {
      if (props[field]) {
        notionProps[field] = { rich_text: [{ text: { content: String(props[field]) } }] };
      }
    }

    const urlFields = ['Perfil LinkedIn', 'LinkedIn Empresa'];
    for (const f of urlFields) {
      if (props[f]) notionProps[f] = { url: props[f] };
    }

    if (props['Telefone']) notionProps['Telefone'] = { phone_number: props['Telefone'] };
    if (props['Mobile'])   notionProps['Mobile']   = { phone_number: props['Mobile'] };
    if (props['Email'])    notionProps['Email']    = { email: props['Email'] };

    const selectFields = ['Como Chegou', 'Origem Lead', 'Conta de Origem'];
    for (const f of selectFields) {
      if (props[f]) notionProps[f] = { select: { name: props[f] } };
    }

    if (props['NCDA Assinado'] !== undefined)   notionProps['NCDA Assinado']   = { checkbox: !!props['NCDA Assinado'] };
    if (props['WhatsApp Criado'] !== undefined)  notionProps['WhatsApp Criado']  = { checkbox: !!props['WhatsApp Criado'] };

    if (props['Status'])      notionProps['Status']      = { select: { name: props['Status'] } };
    if (props['Perfil'])      notionProps['Perfil']      = { select: { name: props['Perfil'] } };
    if (props['Responsavel']) notionProps['Responsavel'] = { select: { name: props['Responsavel'] } };

    if (props['Commodity de Interesse']) {
      const commodities = JSON.parse(props['Commodity de Interesse']);
      notionProps['Commodity de Interesse'] = {
        multi_select: commodities.map(function(name) { return { name: name }; })
      };
    }

    if (props['date:Data Primeiro Contato:start']) {
      notionProps['Data Primeiro Contato'] = {
        date: { start: props['date:Data Primeiro Contato:start'] }
      };
    }
    if (props['date:Data Ultimo Contato:start']) {
      notionProps['Data Ultimo Contato'] = {
        date: { start: props['date:Data Ultimo Contato:start'] }
      };
    }

    const leadName = notionProps['Nome do Lead']?.title?.[0]?.text?.content || '';
    const forceCreate = req.body.force === true;

    // --- Duplicate check (skip if force flag set) ---
    if (leadName && leadName !== 'Lead sem nome' && !forceCreate) {
      const queryRes = await fetch(NOTION_QUERY, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Notion-Version': '2022-06-28',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          filter: {
            property: 'Nome do Lead',
            title: { equals: leadName }
          },
          page_size: 1,
        }),
      });

      if (queryRes.ok) {
        const queryData = await queryRes.json();
        if (queryData.results && queryData.results.length > 0) {
          const existing = queryData.results[0];
          return res.status(409).json({
            duplicate: true,
            existing_id: existing.id,
            existing_url: existing.url,
            existing_name: leadName,
          });
        }
      }
    }

    // --- Create page ---
    const response = await fetch(NOTION_API, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Notion-Version': '2022-06-28',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        parent: { database_id: DATABASE_ID },
        properties: notionProps,
      }),
    });

    const data = await response.json();

    if (!response.ok) {
      const notionMsg = data.message || 'Erro na API do Notion';
      const friendlyError = data.code === 'object_not_found'
        ? 'Banco de dados nao encontrado. Verifique se o database do Notion esta compartilhado com a integracao.'
        : notionMsg;
      return res.status(502).json({
        error: friendlyError,
        code: data.code,
        notion_status: response.status,
      });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ url: data.url, id: data.id });

  } catch (error) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: error.message });
  }
}

tasks.js:

import { MongoClient, ServerApiVersion } from 'mongodb';
import { requireAuth } from './_auth.js';

const clientOptions = {
  serverApi: { version: ServerApiVersion.v1, strict: false, deprecationErrors: false },
  tls: true,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 10000,
  connectTimeoutMS: 10000,
};

let cachedClient = null;

async function getClient() {
  if (cachedClient?.topology?.isConnected()) return cachedClient;
  cachedClient = null;
  const client = new MongoClient(process.env.MONGODB_URI, clientOptions);
  await client.connect();
  cachedClient = client;
  return client;
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (!requireAuth(req, res)) return;

  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, PATCH, DELETE, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();

  try {
    const client = await getClient();
    const db = client.db('samba');
    const col = db.collection('tasks');

    // GET — listar todas as tasks
    if (req.method === 'GET') {
      const items = await col
        .find({})
        .sort({ ts: -1 })
        .limit(200)
        .toArray();
      return res.status(200).json(items);
    }

    // POST — criar task
    if (req.method === 'POST') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      if (!body.ts || !body.subject) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Parâmetros inválidos' });
      await col.insertOne(body);
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    // PATCH — atualizar status ou read
    if (req.method === 'PATCH') {
      const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
      const { ts, ...fields } = body;
      if (!ts) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'ts obrigatório' });
      await col.updateOne({ ts: Number(ts) }, { $set: fields });
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    // DELETE — remover task pelo ts
    if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
      const { ts } = req.query;
      if (!ts) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'ts obrigatório' });
      await col.deleteOne({ ts: Number(ts) });
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
    }

    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Método não permitido' });

  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno', message: err.message });
  }
}

login.js:

import { signToken, cookieHeader } from '../_auth.js';

const ALLOWED_DOMAIN = 'sambaexport.com.br';

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();
  if (req.method !== 'POST') return res.status(405).end();

  try {
    const body = typeof req.body === 'string' ? JSON.parse(req.body) : req.body;
    const { credential } = body || {};
    if (!credential) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Token ausente' });

    // Verify ID token with Google
    const gRes = await fetch(`https://oauth2.googleapis.com/tokeninfo?id_token=${credential}`);
    const payload = await gRes.json();

    if (!gRes.ok || payload.error) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token Google inválido' });
    }
    if (payload.email_verified !== 'true' && payload.email_verified !== true) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'E-mail não verificado pelo Google' });
    }
    if (payload.aud !== process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token não pertence a esta aplicação' });
    }
    if (!payload.email?.endsWith(`@${ALLOWED_DOMAIN}`)) {
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: `Acesso permitido somente para e-mails @${ALLOWED_DOMAIN}`
      });
    }

    const token = signToken({
      email: payload.email,
      name: payload.name,
      picture: payload.picture,
      exp: Date.now() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 8 horas
    });

    res.setHeader('Set-Cookie', cookieHeader(token));
    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Auth login error:', err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Erro interno' });
  }
}

logout.js:

import { cookieHeader } from '../_auth.js';

export default function handler(req, res) {
  res.setHeader('Set-Cookie', cookieHeader(null));
  res.status(200).json({ success: true });
}

me.js:

import { requireAuth } from '../_auth.js';

export default function handler(req, res) {
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();

  const user = requireAuth(req, res);
  if (!user) return;
  res.status(200).json({ email: user.email, name: user.name, picture: user.picture });
}
